   // 不在客户端上设置全局超时，改由每个请求独立控制\n                    .tcp_keepalive_interval(Some(Duration::from_secs(http2_keepalive_secs)))\n                    .tcp_keepalive(Some(Duration::from_secs(tcp_keepalive_secs)))\n                    .pool_idle_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(tcp_keepalive_secs)))\n                    .pool_max_idle_per_host(pool_idle_max)\n                    .build()\n                    .expect(\"构建 MiniMax HTTP 客户端失败\")\n            })\n            .clone();\n        Self { config, http_client }\n    }\n\n    /// 访问配置\n    pub fn config(&self) -> &MiniMaxConfig {\n        &self.config\n    }\n\n    /// 通过 HTTP 调用 MiniMax TTS 并返回音频块流。\n    ///\n    /// `virtual_voice_id` 会被映射到声音库中配置的实际 `voice_id` 与 API key。\n    #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]\n    pub async fn synthesize_text(\n        &self,\n        virtual_voice_id: &str,\n        text: &str,\n        voice_setting: Option<VoiceSetting>,\n        audio_setting: Option<AudioSetting>,\n        pronunciation_dict: Option<PronunciationDict>,\n        timbre_weights: Option<Vec<TimbreWeight>>,\n        language_boost: Option<String>,\n        options: MiniMaxHttpOptions,\n    ) -> Result<Pin<Box<dyn Stream<Item = Result<AudioChunk, MiniMaxError>> + Send + '_>>, MiniMaxError> {\n        if text.trim().is_empty() {\n            return Err(MiniMaxError::Config(\"文本内容不能为空\".to_string()));\n        }\n\n        let (api_key, actual_voice_id) = self\n            .config\n            .get_voice_from_library(virtual_voice_id)\n            .ok_or_else(|| MiniMaxError::Config(format!(\"声音库未找到虚拟 voice_id: {}\", virtual_voice_id)))?;\n\n        let mut voice_setting = voice_setting.unwrap_or_default();\n        voice_setting.voice_id = Some(actual_voice_id.clone());\n\n        // 从声音库读取该 voice_id 的自定义语速和声调配置\n        if let Some(speed) = global_voice_library().get_speed(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.speed = Some(speed);\n        }\n        if let Some(pitch) = global_voice_library().get_pitch(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.pitch = Some(pitch);\n        }\n\n        // 从声音库读取该 voice_id 的模型配置，未配置时使用全局默认模型\n        let model = global_voice_library()\n            .get_model(virtual_voice_id)\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| self.config.model.clone());\n\n        // 从声音库读取该 voice_id 的情绪配置\n        if let Some(emotion) = global_voice_library().get_emotion(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.emotion = Some(emotion);\n        }\n\n        // 从声音库读取该 voice_id 的音量配置\n        if let Some(vol) = global_voice_library().get_vol(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.vol = Some(vol);\n        }\n\n        // 🔧 构造 stream_options（如果需要）\n        let stream_options = if options.exclude_aggregated_audio.is_some() {\n            Some(StreamOptions { exclude_aggregated_audio: options.exclude_aggregated_audio })\n        } else {\n            None\n        };\n\n        // 规范化 language_boost 到 MiniMax 允许的取值\n        let normalized_language_boost = language_boost.as_deref().map(|s| normalize_minimax_lang(Some(s)));\n\n        let request_body = HttpTtsRequest {\n            model,\n            text: text.to_string(),\n            stream: options.stream,\n            voice_setting,\n            audio_setting,\n            pronunciation_dict,\n            timbre_weights,\n            language_boost: normalized_language_boost,\n            voice_modify: options.voice_modify,\n            subtitle_enable: options.subtitle_enable,\n            output_format: options.output_format,\n            aigc_watermark: options.aigc_watermark,\n            stream_options,\n        };\n\n        let mut headers = HeaderMap::new();\n        headers.insert(CONTENT_TYPE, HeaderValue::from_static(\"application/json\"));\n        headers.insert(\n            \"Authorization\",\n            HeaderValue::from_str(&format!(\"Bearer {}\", api_key)).map_err(|err| MiniMaxError::Auth(err.to_string()))?,\n        );\n\n        info!(\n            \"发送 MiniMax HTTP 请求: voice_id={}, model={}, stream={}, exclude_aggregated_audio={:?}, language_boost={:?}\",\n            actual_voice_id,\n            request_body.model,\n            request_body.stream,\n            request_body.stream_options.as_ref().and_then(|so| so.exclude_aggregated_audio),\n            request_body.language_boost\n        );\n\n        let response = self\n            .http_client\n            .post(&self.config.http_url)\n            .headers(headers)\n            .json(&request_body)\n            .timeout(self.config.timeout())\n            .send()\n            .await?\n            .error_for_status()?;\n\n        let status = response.status();\n        debug!(\"MiniMax HTTP 响应状态: {}\", status);\n\n        let body_text = response.text().await?;\n        let response_items = parse_http_response_items(&body_text)?;\n\n        // 从 voice_library 获取该 voice_id 对应的增益（未配置时默认 0.0）\n        let gain_db = global_voice_library().get_gain_db(virtual_voice_id);\n        debug!(\"MiniMax HTTP TTS gain_db for voice_id '{}': {}dB\", virtual_voice_id, gain_db);\n\n        let stream = try_stream! {\n            let mut sequence_id: u64 = 0;\n\n            for item in response_items {\n                if !item.base_resp.is_success() {\n                    let message = item.base_resp.error_message();\n                    warn!(\"MiniMax HTTP 音频块返回错误: {}\", message);\n                    Err(MiniMaxError::Api(message))?;\n                }\n\n                if let Some(data) = item.data {\n                    let status = data.status.unwrap_or_default();\n\n                    if let Some(audio_hex) = data.audio {\n                        let audio_bytes = decode_hex_audio(&audio_hex)?;\n                        let is_final = status == 2;\n                        debug!(\"MiniMax HTTP 收到音频块: status={}, bytes={}, final={}\", status, audio_bytes.len(), is_final);\n\n                        // 🔧 通过 exclude_aggregated_audio=true，API 已确保不会重复发送拼接音频\n                        // 使用从 voice_library 获取的增益值，MiniMax 输出 44100Hz\n                        let chunk = AudioChunk::new_with_gain(audio_bytes, sequence_id, is_final, gain_db);\n                        sequence_id = sequence_id.saturating_add(1);\n                        yield chunk;\n                    } else if status == 2 {\n                        debug!(\"MiniMax HTTP 收到最终块但无音频数据，补发空控制块\");\n                        let chunk = AudioChunk::new_with_gain(Vec::new(), sequence_id, true, gain_db);\n                        sequence_id = sequence_id.saturating_add(1);\n                        yield chunk;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if let Some(extra) = item.extra_info {\n                    debug!(\n                        \"MiniMax HTTP extra_info: duration={}ms, sample_rate={:?}, format={:?}\",\n                        extra.audio_length.unwrap_or_default(),\n                        extra.audio_sample_rate,\n                        extra.audio_format\n                    );\n                }\n            }\n\n            // 为了保持与 WS 客户端一致，追加 session 级别的 final 控制块\n            debug!(\"MiniMax HTTP 补发会话级 final 控制块\");\n            let final_chunk = AudioChunk::new_with_gain(Vec::new(), u64::MAX, true, gain_db);\n            yield final_chunk;\n        };\n\n        Ok(Box::pin(stream))\n    }\n\n    /// 使用 HEAD 预热与服务端的 HTTP 连接，失败时回退 GET\n    pub async fn prewarm_connection(&self) -> anyhow::Result<()> {\n        let endpoint = self.config.http_url.clone();\n        // 尝试从默认voice获取一个API key（若无则不携带Authorization也可完成握手）\n        let mut headers = HeaderMap::new();\n        headers.insert(CONTENT_TYPE, HeaderValue::from_static(\"application/json\"));\n        if let Some(ref vid) = self.config.default_voice_id\n            && let Some((api_key, _)) = self.config.get_voice_from_library(vid)\n            && let Ok(value) = HeaderValue::from_str(&format!(\"Bearer {}\", api_key))\n        {\n            headers.insert(\"Authorization\", value);\n        }\n\n        // 🔧 优化：减少 prewarm 超时时间，避免长时间阻塞初始化流程\n        // 原先 HEAD 5s + GET 5s = 10s，现改为 HEAD 2s + GET 2s = 4s\n        let head_result = self\n            .http_client\n            .head(endpoint.clone())\n            .headers(headers.clone())\n            .timeout(Duration::from_secs(2))\n            .send()\n            .await;\n\n        if head_result.is_ok() {\n            info!(\"🔥 MiniMax HTTP 连接已预热 (HEAD)\");\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n\n        let get_result = self\n            .http_client\n            .get(endpoint)\n            .headers(headers)\n            .timeout(Duration::from_secs(2))\n            .send()\n            .await;\n\n        match get_result {\n            Ok(_) => {\n                info!(\"🔥 MiniMax HTTP 连接已预热 (GET fallback)\");\n                Ok(())\n            },\n            Err(e) => {\n                warn!(\"⚠️ MiniMax 连接预热失败 (HEAD+GET): {}\", e);\n                Err(anyhow::anyhow!(e))\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// 并发预热多条连接\n    pub async fn prewarm_connections(&self, count: usize) -> anyhow::Result<()> {\n        if count <= 1 {\n            return self.prewarm_connection().await;\n        }\n        let endpoint = self.config.http_url.clone();\n        let mut headers = HeaderMap::new();\n        headers.insert(CONTENT_TYPE, HeaderValue::from_static(\"application/json\"));\n        if let Some(ref vid) = self.config.default_voice_id\n            && let Some((api_key, _)) = self.config.get_voice_from_library(vid)\n            && let Ok(value) = HeaderValue::from_str(&format!(\"Bearer {}\", api_key))\n        {\n            headers.insert(\"Authorization\", value);\n        }\n\n        let mut tasks = Vec::with_capacity(count);\n        for _ in 0..count {\n            let client = self.http_client.clone();\n            let endpoint_cloned = endpoint.clone();\n            let headers_cloned = headers.clone();\n            // 🔧 优化：减少并发 prewarm 超时时间至 2s\n            tasks.push(tokio::spawn(async move {\n                if client\n                    .head(endpoint_cloned.clone())\n                    .headers(headers_cloned.clone())\n                    .timeout(Duration::from_secs(2))\n                    .send()\n                    .await\n                    .is_err()\n                {\n                    let _ = client\n                        .get(endpoint_cloned)\n                        .headers(headers_cloned)\n                        .timeout(Duration::from_secs(2))\n                        .send()\n                        .await;\n                }\n            }));\n        }\n        for t in tasks {\n            let _ = t.await;\n        }\n        info!(\"🔥 MiniMax 连接并发预热完成\");\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\nfn decode_hex_audio(hex_str: &str) -> Result<Vec<u8>, MiniMaxError> {\n    hex::decode(hex_str).map_err(|err| MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\"音频数据hex解码失败: {}\", err)))\n}\n\nfn parse_http_response_items(body: &str) -> Result<Vec<HttpTtsResponseItem>, MiniMaxError> {\n    let trimmed = body.trim();\n    if trimmed.is_empty() {\n        return Err(MiniMaxError::Other(\"MiniMax HTTP 响应为空\".to_string()));\n    }\n\n    if trimmed.starts_with('[') {\n        return serde_json::from_str::<Vec<HttpTtsResponseItem>>(trimmed).map_err(|err| MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\"MiniMax HTTP 响应解析失败: {}\", err)));\n    }\n\n    if trimmed.starts_with(\"data:\") {\n        let mut items: Vec<HttpTtsResponseItem> = Vec::new();\n        for block in trimmed.split(\"\\n\\n\") {\n            let mut data_lines: Vec<&str> = Vec::new();\n            for line in block.lines() {\n                if let Some(rest) = line.strip_prefix(\"data:\") {\n                    let payload = rest.trim();\n                    if payload.is_empty() || payload == \"[DONE]\" {\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    data_lines.push(payload);\n                }\n            }\n            if data_lines.is_empty() {\n                continue;\n            }\n            let payload = data_lines.join(\"\\n\");\n            match serde_json::from_str::<HttpTtsResponseItem>(&payload) {\n                Ok(item) => items.push(item),\n                Err(err) => {\n                    return Err(MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\n                        \"MiniMax HTTP SSE 响应解析失败: {}。原始片段前128字节: {}\",\n                        err,\n                        payload.chars().take(128).collect::<String>()\n                    )));\n                },\n            }\n        }\n        if items.is_empty() {\n            return Err(MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\n                \"MiniMax HTTP SSE 响应为空: {}\",\n                trimmed.chars().take(128).collect::<String>()\n            )));\n        }\n        return Ok(items);\n    }\n\n    let mut items = Vec::new();\n    let deserializer = Deserializer::from_str(trimmed).into_iter::<HttpTtsResponseItem>();\n    let mut index = 0usize;\n    for result in deserializer {\n        index += 1;\n        match result {\n            Ok(item) => items.push(item),\n            Err(err) => {\n                return Err(MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\n                    \"MiniMax HTTP 流式响应解析失败 (entry {}): {}。原始片段前128字节: {}\",\n                    index,\n                    err,\n                    trimmed.chars().take(128).collect::<String>()\n                )));\n            },\n        }\n    }\n    if items.is_empty() {\n        return Err(MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\n            \"MiniMax HTTP 响应格式未知: {}\",\n            trimmed.chars().take(128).collect::<String>()\n        )));\n    }\n    Ok(items)\n}\n\n/// 流式选项配置\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\nstruct StreamOptions {\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    exclude_aggregated_audio: Option<bool>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Serialize)]\nstruct HttpTtsRequest {\n    model: String,\n    text: String,\n    stream: bool,\n    voice_setting: VoiceSetting,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    audio_setting: Option<AudioSetting>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    pronunciation_dict: Option<PronunciationDict>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    timbre_weights: Option<Vec<TimbreWeight>>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    language_boost: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    voice_modify: Option<serde_json::Value>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    subtitle_enable: Option<bool>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    output_format: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    aigc_watermark: Option<bool>,\n    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = \"Option::is_none\")]\n    stream_options: Option<StreamOptions>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct HttpTtsResponseItem {\n    #[serde(default)]\n    data: Option<HttpTtsResponseData>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    extra_info: Option<ExtraInfo>,\n    #[serde(rename = \"base_resp\")]\n    base_resp: BaseResponse,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)]\nstruct HttpTtsResponseData {\n    #[serde(default)]\n    audio: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    status: Option<i32>,\n}\n"
  }
}
```

    "output": "//! Voice Session Actor\n//!\n//! 1 会话 = 1 Actor，通过 tokio::mpsc 驱动，无共享状态。\n//!\n//! 外部通过 VoiceSession 发送命令，内部独立运行 TTS / ASR 任务。\n//! 中断通过替换 GenerationHandle 实现（旧 handle drop = 旧任务 abort）。\n\npub mod interrupt;\npub mod router;\n\nuse tokio::sync::mpsc;\nuse tokio_util::sync::CancellationToken;\nuse tracing::{debug, error, info};\n\nuse crate::pipeline::frame::{AudioFrame, ControlFrame, Frame};\nuse interrupt::{GenerationHandle, InterruptEngine};\n\n/// 发给 Session Actor 的命令\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub enum SessionCommand {\n    /// TTS：将文本合成语音并播放\n    Speak(SpeakRequest),\n    /// 中断当前 TTS 输出\n    Interrupt,\n    /// 外部帧输入（来自麦克风/ASR）\n    Frame(Frame),\n    /// 关闭 session\n    Shutdown,\n    /// 内部：TTS 任务自然结束（用于重置 current_priority）\n    SpeechFinished,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct SpeakRequest {\n    /// 要朗读的文本\n    pub text: String,\n    /// TTS 引擎类型\n    pub engine: TtsEngine,\n    /// 优先级高的请求会自动中断低优先级的\n    pub priority: u8,\n    /// SSML prosody 语速（如 \"+10%\"），None 使用引擎默认值\n    pub rate: Option<String>,\n    /// SSML prosody 音高（如 \"+5Hz\"），None 使用引擎默认值\n    pub pitch: Option<String>,\n    /// SSML prosody 音量（如 \"+10%\"），None 使用引擎默认值\n    pub self.priority = p;\n        self\n    }\n    pub fn with_rate(mut self, rate: impl Into<String>) -> Self {\n        self.rate = Some(rate.into());\n        self\n    }\n    pub fn with_pitch(mut self, Some(volume.into());\n        self\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum TtsEngine {\n    Edge,\n    MiniMax { api_key: String, voice_id: String },\n    Azure { subscription_key: String, region: String },\n}\n\n/// Session 产出的事件（可订阅）\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum SessionEvent {\n    /// TTS 音频帧（可直接播放）\n    AudioReady(AudioFrame),\n    /// TTS 开始\n    SpeechStart { text: String },\n    /// TTS 完成\n    SpeechEnd,\n    /// TTS 被中断\n    SpeechInterrupted,\n    /// ASR 转写结果\n    Transcript { text: String, is_final: bool },\n    /// Session 已关闭\n    Closed,\n}\n\n/// Voice Session 的客户端句柄\n///\n/// Clone 后多处持有，共享同一个 actor。\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct VoiceSession {\n    cmd_tx: mpsc::Sender<SessionCommand>,\n    event_tx: tokio::sync::broadcast::Sender<SessionEvent>,\n}\n\nimpl VoiceSession {\n    /// 创建新的 Session，返回句柄和后台 actor 的 JoinHandle\n    pub fn spawn(config: SessionConfig) -> (Self, tokio::task::JoinHandle<()>) {\n        let (cmd_tx, cmd_rx) = mpsc::channel(64);\n        let (event_tx, _) = tokio::sync::broadcast::channel(128);\n        let event_tx_clone = event_tx.clone();\n\n        let session = Self { cmd_tx, event_tx };\n\n        let cmd_tx_inner = session.cmd_tx.clone();\n        let handle = tokio::spawn(async move {\n            SessionActor::new(config, cmd_tx_inner, cmd_rx, event_tx_clone).run().await;\n        });\n\n        (session, handle)\n    }\n\n    /// 合成并播放文本\n    pub async fn speak(&self, req: SpeakRequest) -> Result<(), SessionError> {\n        self.cmd_tx.send(SessionCommand::Speak(req)).await.map_err(|_| SessionError::SessionClosed)\n    }\n\n    /// 中断当前 TTS\n    pub async fn interrupt(&self) -> Result<(), SessionError> {\n        self.cmd_tx.send(SessionCommand::Interrupt).await.map_err(|_| SessionError::SessionClosed)\n    }\n\n    /// 推送外部帧（麦克风音频等）\n    pub async fn push_frame(&self, frame: Frame) -> Result<(), SessionError> {\n        self.cmd_tx.send(SessionCommand::Frame(frame)).await.map_err(|_| SessionError::SessionClosed)\n    }\n\n    /// 关闭 session\n    pub async fn shutdown(&self) {\n        let _ = self.cmd_tx.send(SessionCommand::Shutdown).await;\n    }\n\n    /// 订阅 session 事件\n    pub fn subscribe(&self) -> tokio::sync::broadcast::Receiver<SessionEvent> {\n        self.event_tx.subscribe()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Session 配置\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct SessionConfig {\n    pub session_id: String,\n    /// TTS 输出 channel 缓冲大小\n    pub audio_buffer: usize,\n    /// Edge TTS 声音名称（如 \"zh-CN-XiaoxiaoNeural\"）\n    pub tts_voice: String,\n}\n\nimpl Default for SessionConfig {\n    fn default() -> Self {\n        Self {\n            session_id: uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string(),\n            audio_buffer: 32,\n            tts_voice: \"zh-CN-XiaoxiaoNeural\".to_string(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]\npub enum SessionError {\n    #[error(\"session is closed\")]\n    SessionClosed,\n    #[error(\"tts error: {0}\")]\n    Tts(String),\n}\n\n/// 内部 Actor：持有所有可变状态\nstruct SessionActor {\n    config: SessionConfig,\n    cmd_tx: mpsc::Sender<SessionCommand>,\n    cmd_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SessionCommand>,\n    event_tx: tokio::sync::broadcast::Sender<SessionEvent>,\n    interrupt: InterruptEngine,\n    /// 当前 TTS 任务的句柄（replace 即可中断旧任务）\n    current_generation: Option<GenerationHandle>,\n    /// 当前正在播放的 TTS 优先级（用于抢占判断）\n    current_priority: u8,\n    #[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\n    edge_client: crate::tts::EdgeTtsClient,\n}\n\nimpl SessionActor {\n    fn new(\n        config: SessionConfig,\n        cmd_tx: mpsc::Sender<SessionCommand>,\n        cmd_rx: mpsc::Receiver<SessionCommand>,\n        event_tx: tokio::sync::broadcast::Sender<SessionEvent>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        #[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\n        let edge_client = crate::tts::EdgeTtsClient::new(\n            crate::tts::EdgeTtsConfig::default().with_voice(&config.tts_voice),\n        );\n        Self {\n            config,\n            cmd_tx,\n            cmd_rx,\n            event_tx,\n            interrupt: InterruptEngine::new(),\n            current_generation: None,\n            current_priority: 0,\n            #[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\n            edge_client,\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn run(mut self) {\n        info!(\"session {} started\", self.config.session_id);\n\n        while let Some(cmd) = self.cmd_rx.recv().await {\n            match cmd {\n                SessionCommand::Speak(req) => self.handle_speak(req),\n                SessionCommand::Interrupt => self.handle_interrupt(),\n                SessionCommand::Frame(frame) => self.handle_frame(frame).await,\n                SessionCommand::SpeechFinished => {\n                    self.current_generation = None;\n                    self.current_priority = 0;\n                }\n                SessionCommand::Shutdown => {\n                    info!(\"session {} shutting down\", self.config.session_id);\n                    let _ = self.event_tx.send(SessionEvent::Closed);\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn handle_speak(&mut self, req: SpeakRequest) {\n        // 优先级抢占：新请求优先级 >= 当前才允许打断\n        // 低优先级请求在当前播放期间被丢弃（避免队列堆积）\n        if self.current_generation.is_some() && req.priority < self.current_priority {\n            debug!(\n                \"speak request priority {} < current {}, discarded\",\n                req.priority, self.current_priority\n            );\n            return;\n        }\n\n        let priority = req.priority;\n        let text = req.text.clone();\n        let event_tx = self.event_tx.clone();\n        let cmd_tx = self.cmd_tx.clone();\n        #[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\n        let edge_client = {\n            if req.rate.is_some() || req.pitch.is_some() || req.volume.is_some() {\n                self.edge_client.with_prosody_override(req.rate.clone(), req.pitch.clone(), req.volume.clone())\n            } else {\n                self.edge_client.clone()\n            }\n        };\n\n        let _ = event_tx.send(SessionEvent::SpeechStart { text: text.clone() });\n\n        let handle = self.interrupt.start(move |cancel_token| async move {\n            #[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\n            Self::run_tts(text, req.engine, edge_client, cancel_token, event_tx).await;\n            #[cfg(not(feature = \"tts\"))]\n            {\n                let _ = (text, req.engine, cancel_token);\n                let _ = event_tx.send(SessionEvent::SpeechEnd);\n            }\n            // 通知 Actor 自然结束，重置 current_priority\n            let _ = cmd_tx.try_send(SessionCommand::SpeechFinished);\n        });\n\n        self.current_generation = Some(handle);\n        self.current_priority = priority;\n    }\n\n    fn handle_interrupt(&mut self) {\n        if self.current_generation.is_some() {\n            debug!(\"session interrupt: dropping generation handle\");\n            self.current_generation = None; // drop = abort\n            self.current_priority = 0;\n            let _ = self.event_tx.send(SessionEvent::SpeechInterrupted);\n        }\n    }\n\n    async fn handle_frame(&mut self, frame: Frame) {\n        // VAD 检测到语音开始 → 自动中断当前 TTS\n        if let Frame::Control(ControlFrame::SpeechStart) = &frame {\n            self.handle_interrupt();\n        }\n        // 其他帧交给 pipeline 处理（后续扩展）\n    }\n\n    /// TTS 任务的实际执行逻辑（仅在 tts feature 启用时编译）\n    ///\n    /// 按句子流式合成，每句合成完立即发送 AudioReady，\n    /// 每次合成前检查 cancel_token 实现零延迟中断。\n    #[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\n    async fn run_tts(\n        text: String,\n        engine: TtsEngine,\n        edge_client: crate::tts::EdgeTtsClient,\n        cancel_token: CancellationToken,\n        event_tx: tokio::sync::broadcast::Sender<SessionEvent>,\n    ) {\n        let sentences = split_sentences(&text);\n\n        for sentence in sentences {\n            if cancel_token.is_cancelled() {\n                debug!(\"tts cancelled before sentence: {}\", sentence);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            tokio::select! {\n                _ = cancel_token.cancelled() => {\n                    debug!(\"tts interrupted mid-sentence\");\n                    return;\n                }\n                result = synthesize_sentence(&sentence, &engine, &edge_client) => {\n                    match result {\n                        Ok(audio) => {\n                            let _ = event_tx.send(SessionEvent::AudioReady(audio));\n                        }\n                        Err(e) => {\n                            error!(\"tts error: {}\", e);\n                            return;\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        let _ = event_tx.send(SessionEvent::SpeechEnd);\n    }\n}\n\n/// 按标点分句（简化实现，后续可接 text_splitter 模块）\nfn split_sentences(text: &str) -> Vec<String> {\n    let mut sentences = Vec::new();\n    let mut current = String::new();\n\n    for ch in text.chars() {\n        current.push(ch);\n        if matches!(ch, '。' | '！' | '？' | '…' | '.' | '!' | '?') {\n            let s = current.trim().to_string();\n            if !s.is_empty() {\n                sentences.push(s);\n            }\n            current.clear();\n        }\n    }\n\n    let remaining = current.trim().to_string();\n    if !remaining.is_empty() {\n        sentences.push(remaining);\n    }\n\n    if sentences.is_empty() && !text.is_empty() {\n        sentences.push(text.to_string());\n    }\n\n    sentences\n}\n\n/// 单句 TTS 合成：收集流式 PCM 块后合并为一个 AudioFrame\n#[cfg(feature = \"tts\")]\nasync fn synthesize_sentence(\n    text: &str,\n    engine: &TtsEngine,\n    edge_client: &crate::tts::EdgeTtsClient,\n) -> Result<AudioFrame, String> {\n    use futures_util::StreamExt as _;\n\n    match engine {\n        TtsEngine::Edge => {\n            let mut stream = edge_client.synthesize(text, None).await.map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;\n\n            let mut pcm: Vec<u8> = Vec::new();\n            let mut sample_rate = 16000u32;\n\n            while let Some(chunk) = stream.next().await {\n                match chunk {\n                    Ok(c) => {\n                        if c.is_final {\n                            break;\n                        }\n                        sample_rate = c.sample_rate;\n                        pcm.extend_from_slice(&c.data);\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => return Err(e.to_string()),\n                }\n            }\n\n            Ok(AudioFrame::new_pcm16(bytes::Bytes::from(pcm), sample_rate))\n        }\n        TtsEngine::MiniMax { .. } => {\n            // TODO: 接入 MiniMaxHttpTtsClient\n            Ok(AudioFrame::new_pcm16(bytes::Bytes::new(), 16000))\n        }\n        TtsEngine::Azure { .. } => {\n            // TODO: 接入 AzureTtsClient\n            Ok(AudioFrame::new_pcm16(bytes::Bytes::new(), 16000))\n        }\n    }\n}\n"
  }
}
```

    "output": "//! MiniMax TTS WebSocket 客户端\n//!\n//! 通过 WebSocket 连接 MiniMax TTS 服务（wss://api.minimaxi.com/ws/v1/t2a_v2），\n//! 使用 task_start / task_continue / task_finish 协议进行流式语音合成。\n//!\n//! 协议流程：\n//!   1. 建立 WebSocket 连接（Authorization: Bearer 头）\n//!   2. 发送 task_start → 接收 connected_success / task_started\n//!   3. 发送 task_continue(text) → 接收 task_continued（含 base64 音频）\n//!   4. 发送 task_finish → 接收 task_finished\n\nuse std::pin::Pin;\n\nuse async_stream::try_stream;\nuse base64::Engine as _;\nuse futures_util::{SinkExt, Stream, StreamExt};\nuse tokio_tungstenite::tungstenite::Message;\nuse tracing::{debug, warn};\n\nuse super::config::MiniMaxConfig;\nuse super::types::{\n    AudioSetting, MiniMaxError, TaskContinueRequest, TaskFinishRequest, TaskStartRequest,\n    VoiceSetting, WebSocketResponse,\n};\nuse super::voice_library::global_voice_library;\nuse super::AudioChunk;\n\n/// MiniMax TTS WebSocket 客户端\n#[derive(Clone)]\npub struct MiniMaxWsTtsClient {\n    config: MiniMaxConfig,\n}\n\nimpl MiniMaxWsTtsClient {\n    pub fn new(config: MiniMaxConfig) -> Self {\n        Self { config }\n    }\n\n    pub fn with_defaults() -> Self {\n        Self::new(MiniMaxConfig::default())\n    }\n\n    /// 合成单句文本，返回 PCM 音频块流。\n    ///\n    /// `virtual_voice_id` 通过声音库映射到实际的 voice_id 和 API key。\n    pub fn synthesize(\n        &self,\n        virtual_voice_id: &str,\n        text: &str,\n        voice_setting: Option<VoiceSetting>,\n        audio_setting: Option<AudioSetting>,\n    ) -> Result<Pin<Box<dyn Stream<Item = Result<AudioChunk, MiniMaxError>> + Send + 'static>>, MiniMaxError>\n    {\n        if text.trim().is_empty() {\n            return Err(MiniMaxError::Config(\"文本内容不能为空\".to_string()));\n        }\n\n        let (api_key, actual_voice_id) = self\n            .config\n            .get_voice_from_library(virtual_voice_id)\n            .ok_or_else(|| {\n                MiniMaxError::Config(format!(\"声音库未找到虚拟 voice_id: {}\", virtual_voice_id))\n            })?;\n\n        let mut voice_setting = voice_setting.unwrap_or_default();\n        voice_setting.voice_id = Some(actual_voice_id.clone());\n\n        // 从声音库读取自定义配置\n        if let Some(speed) = global_voice_library().get_speed(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.speed = Some(speed);\n        }\n        if let Some(pitch) = global_voice_library().get_pitch(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.pitch = Some(pitch);\n        }\n        if let Some(emotion) = global_voice_library().get_emotion(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.emotion = Some(emotion);\n        }\n        if let Some(vol) = global_voice_library().get_vol(virtual_voice_id) {\n            voice_setting.vol = Some(vol);\n        }\n\n        let model = global_voice_library()\n            .get_model(virtual_voice_id)\n            .unwrap_or_else(|| self.config.model.clone());\n\n        let audio_setting = audio_setting.unwrap_or_default();\n        let gain_db = global_voice_library().get_gain_db(virtual_voice_id);\n        let ws_url = self.config.ws_url.clone();\n        let text = text.to_string();\n\n        let stream = try_stream! {\n            // 1. 建立 WebSocket 连接\n            let request = tokio_tungstenite::tungstenite::http::Request::builder()\n                .uri(&ws_url)\n                .header(\"Authorization\", format!(\"Bearer {}\", api_key))\n                .body(())\n                .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::WebSocket(format!(\"构建请求失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n            let (ws_stream, _) = tokio_tungstenite::connect_async(request)\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::WebSocket(format!(\"WebSocket 连接失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n            let (mut write, mut read) = ws_stream.split();\n\n            // 2. 发送 task_start\n            let task_start = serde_json::to_string(&TaskStartRequest {\n                event: \"task_start\".to_string(),\n                model: model.clone(),\n                voice_setting: voice_setting.clone(),\n                audio_setting: Some(audio_setting.clone()),\n                pronunciation_dict: None,\n                timbre_weights: None,\n                language_boost: None,\n                voice_modify: None,\n            })\n            .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::Json(e))?;\n\n            write\n                .send(Message::Text(task_start.into()))\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::WebSocket(format!(\"发送 task_start 失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n            debug!(\"MiniMax WS: task_start 已发送\");\n\n            // 3. 发送 task_continue\n            let task_continue = serde_json::to_string(&TaskContinueRequest {\n                event: \"task_continue\".to_string(),\n                text: text.clone(),\n            })\n            .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::Json(e))?;\n\n            write\n                .send(Message::Text(task_continue.into()))\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::WebSocket(format!(\"发送 task_continue 失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n            debug!(\"MiniMax WS: task_continue 已发送\");\n\n            // 4. 发送 task_finish\n            let task_finish = serde_json::to_string(&TaskFinishRequest {\n                event: \"task_finish\".to_string(),\n            })\n            .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::Json(e))?;\n\n            write\n                .send(Message::Text(task_finish.into()))\n                .await\n                .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::WebSocket(format!(\"发送 task_finish 失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n            debug!(\"MiniMax WS: task_finish 已发送\");\n\n            // 5. 读取响应\n            let mut sequence_id: u64 = 0;\n\n            while let Some(msg) = read.next().await {\n                let msg = msg.map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::WebSocket(format!(\"读取消息失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n                let text = match msg {\n                    Message::Text(t) => t.to_string(),\n                    Message::Binary(b) => {\n                        warn!(\"MiniMax WS: 收到意外二进制消息，长度={}\", b.len());\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    Message::Close(_) => {\n                        debug!(\"MiniMax WS: 连接关闭\");\n                        break;\n                    }\n                    Message::Ping(data) => {\n                        let _ = write.send(Message::Pong(data)).await;\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    Message::Pong(_) => continue,\n                    Message::Frame(_) => continue,\n                };\n\n                let response: WebSocketResponse = match serde_json::from_str(&text) {\n                    Ok(r) => r,\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        warn!(\"MiniMax WS: 解析响应失败: {e}, raw={}\", &text[..text.len().min(200)]);\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                };\n\n                match response {\n                    WebSocketResponse::ConnectedSuccess { base_resp, session_id, .. } => {\n                        if !base_resp.is_success() {\n                            Err(MiniMaxError::Api(base_resp.error_message()))?;\n                        }\n                        debug!(\"MiniMax WS: 连接成功, session={}\", session_id);\n                    }\n                    WebSocketResponse::TaskStarted { base_resp, .. } => {\n                        if !base_resp.is_success() {\n                            Err(MiniMaxError::Api(base_resp.error_message()))?;\n                        }\n                        debug!(\"MiniMax WS: 任务已启动\");\n                    }\n                    WebSocketResponse::TaskContinued { data, base_resp, extra_info, .. } => {\n                        if !base_resp.is_success() {\n                            Err(MiniMaxError::Api(base_resp.error_message()))?;\n                        }\n\n                        if let Some(extra) = &extra_info {\n                            debug!(\n                                \"MiniMax WS: extra_info duration={}ms, sample_rate={:?}, format={:?}\",\n                                extra.audio_length.unwrap_or_default(),\n                                extra.audio_sample_rate,\n                                extra.audio_format\n                            );\n                        }\n\n                        if let Some(d) = data {\n                            let audio_bytes = base64::engine::general_purpose::STANDARD\n                                .decode(&d.audio)\n                                .map_err(|e| MiniMaxError::Other(format!(\"base64 解码失败: {e}\")))?;\n\n                            if !audio_bytes.is_empty() {\n                                let chunk = AudioChunk::new_with_gain_and_sample_rate(\n                                    audio_bytes,\n                                    sequence_id,\n                                    false,\n                                    gain_db,\n                                    44100,\n                                );\n                                sequence_id = sequence_id.saturating_add(1);\n                                yield chunk;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                    WebSocketResponse::TaskFinished { base_resp, .. } => {\n                        if !base_resp.is_success() {\n                            Err(MiniMaxError::Api(base_resp.error_message()))?;\n                        }\n                        debug!(\"MiniMax WS: 任务完成\");\n                        break;\n                    }\n                    WebSocketResponse::TaskFailed { base_resp, .. } => {\n                        Err(MiniMaxError::Api(base_resp.error_message()))?;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // 发送最终控制块\n            let final_chunk = AudioChunk::new_with_gain_and_sample_rate(\n                Vec::new(),\n                u64::MAX,\n                true,\n                gain_db,\n                44100,\n            );\n            yield final_chunk;\n\n            let _ = write.close().await;\n        };\n\n        Ok(Box::pin(stream))\n    }\n}\n"
  }
}
